3.855l-5.833-3.387L15.119 7.2a.076.076 0 0 1 .071 0l4.83 2.791a4.494 4.494 0 0 1-.676 8.105v-5.678a.79.79 0 0 0-.407-.667zm2.01-3.023l-.141-.085-4.774-2.782a.776.776 0 0 0-.785 0L9.409 9.23V6.897a.066.066 0 0 1 .028-.061l4.83-2.787a4.5 4.5 0 0 1 6.68 4.66zm-12.64 4.135l-2.02-1.164a.08.08 0 0 1-.038-.057V6.075a4.5 4.5 0 0 1 7.375-3.453l-.142.08L8.704 5.46a.795.795 0 0 002-2v-3a1 1 0 10-2 0v3H5V7h3a1 1 0 000-2H5z"></path></svg></a></div></div></div></div><p>The Collection class is designed to manage a collection of items, providing
functionalities such as sorting, searching, getting next or previous items,
converting items to values or strings, checking if an item is disabled, and
more.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p><strong>Good to know</strong>: This is used in the select and combobox components</p>
</blockquote>
<h2 id="list-collection" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">List Collection<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#list-collection"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>A list collection is a collection that is based on an array of items. It is
created by passing an array of items to the constructor.</p>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> ListCollection <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/collection&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> collection <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">ListCollection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  items<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">{</span> label<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Apple&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> value<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;apple&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">{</span> label<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Banana&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> value<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;banana&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="converting-value-to-item" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Converting value to item<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#converting-value-to-item"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>You can convert a value to an item by passing the value to the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">find</code> or
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">findMany</code> method.</p>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> item <span class="token operator">=</span> collection<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">find</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;banana&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>item<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// { label: &quot;Banana&quot;, value: &quot;banana&quot; }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> items <span class="token operator">=</span> collection<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">findMany</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;apple&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">&quot;banana&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>items<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// [{ label: &quot;Apple&quot;, value: &quot;apple&quot; }, { label: &quot;Banana&quot;, value: &quot;banana&quot; }]</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="value-traversal" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Value Traversal<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#value-traversal"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>You can get the next or previous item based on a value by passing the value to
the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getNextValue</code> or <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getPreviousValue</code> method.</p>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> nextValue <span class="token operator">=</span> collection<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getNextValue</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;apple&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>nextValue<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// banana</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> previousItem <span class="token operator">=</span> collection<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getPreviousValue</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;banana&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>previousItem<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// apple</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>Likewise, you can also get the first or last item by calling the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">firstValue</code> or
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">lastValue</code> computed properties.</p>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>collection<span class="token punctuation">.</span>firstValue<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// apple</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>collection<span class="token punctuation">.</span>lastValue<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// banana</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="check-for-value-existence" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Check for value existence<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#check-for-value-existence"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>You can check if a value exists in the collection by calling the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">has</code> method.</p>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> hasValue <span class="token operator">=</span> collection<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">has</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;apple&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>hasValue<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// true</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="working-with-custom-objects" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Working with custom objects<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#working-with-custom-objects"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>If you are working with custom objects, you can pass a function to the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">itemToString</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getItemValue</code> options to specify how to convert an item to a
string and a value, respectively.</p>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> ListCollection <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/collection&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> collection <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">ListCollection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  items<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">{</span> id<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> name<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;apple&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">{</span> id<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> name<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;banana&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">{</span> id<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> name<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;cherry&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">itemToString</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>item<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> item<span class="token punctuation">.</span>name<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">itemToValue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>item<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> item<span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>To disable an item, you can pass a function to the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">isItemDisabled</code> option.</p>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> ListCollection <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/collection&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> collection <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">ListCollection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  items<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">{</span> id<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> name<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;apple&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">{</span> id<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> name<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;banana&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">{</span> id<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> name<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;cherry&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">isItemDisabled</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>item<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> item<span class="token punctuation">.</span>id <span class="token operator">===</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="reorder-items" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Reorder items<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#reorder-items"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>You can reorder items by calling the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">reorder</code> method and passing the starting
index and the ending index of the item to be moved.</p>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> fromIndex <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">1</span> <span class="token comment">// Banana</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> toIndex <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">0</span> <span class="token comment">// Apple</span>
</span><span class="code-line">collection<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">reorder</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fromIndex<span class="token punctuation">,</span> toIndex<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>collection<span class="token punctuation">.</span>items<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// [{ label: &quot;Banana&quot;, value: &quot;banana&quot; }, { label: &quot;Apple&quot;, value: &quot;apple&quot; }]</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="tree-collection" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Tree Collection<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#tree-collection"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>A tree collection is designed to manage hierarchical data structures like file
systems, navigation menus, or organization charts. It provides powerful methods
for traversing, manipulating, and querying tree structures.</p>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> TreeCollection <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/collection&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> treeData <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  value<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  label<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  children<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      value<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;folder1&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      label<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Folder 1&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      children<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token punctuation">{</span> value<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;file1&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> label<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;File 1.txt&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token punctuation">{</span> value<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;file2&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> label<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;File 2.txt&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      value<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;folder2&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      label<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Folder 2&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      children<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">          value<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;subfolder1&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">          label<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Subfolder 1&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">          children<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> value<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;file3&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> label<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;File 3.txt&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> tree <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">TreeCollection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> rootNode<span class="token operator">:</span> treeData <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="navigation-methods" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Navigation Methods<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#navigation-methods"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The tree collection provides various methods to navigate through the
hierarchical structure.</p>
<h4 id="getting-first-and-last-nodes" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Getting First and Last Nodes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#getting-first-and-last-nodes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> firstNode <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getFirstNode</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>firstNode<span class="token operator">?.</span>value<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// &quot;folder1&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> lastNode <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getLastNode</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lastNode<span class="token operator">?.</span>value<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// &quot;folder2&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="sequential-navigation" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Sequential Navigation<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#sequential-navigation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>Navigate to the next or previous node in the tree traversal order:</p>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> nextNode <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getNextNode</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;file1&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>nextNode<span class="token operator">?.</span>value<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// &quot;file2&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> previousNode <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getPreviousNode</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;file2&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>previousNode<span class="token operator">?.</span>value<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// &quot;file1&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="hierarchical-relationships" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Hierarchical Relationships<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#hierarchical-relationships"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<h4 id="parent-and-children" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Parent and Children<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#parent-and-children"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>Get parent and descendant nodes:</p>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Get parent node</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> parentNode <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getParentNode</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;file1&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>parentNode<span class="token operator">?.</span>value<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// &quot;folder1&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Get all ancestor nodes</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> ancestors <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getParentNodes</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;file3&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>ancestors<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">map</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>n<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> n<span class="token punctuation">.</span>value<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// [&quot;folder2&quot;, &quot;subfolder1&quot;]</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Get all descendant nodes</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> descendants <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getDescendantNodes</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;folder1&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>descendants<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">map</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>n<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> n<span class="token punctuation">.</span>value<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// [&quot;file1&quot;, &quot;file2&quot;]</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Get descendant values only</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> descendantValues <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getDescendantValues</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;folder2&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>descendantValues<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// [&quot;subfolder1&quot;, &quot;file3&quot;]</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="sibling-navigation" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Sibling Navigation<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#sibling-navigation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>Navigate between sibling nodes:</p>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Assuming we have the index path of &quot;file1&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> indexPath <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getIndexPath</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;file1&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// [0, 0]</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> nextSibling <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getNextSibling</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>indexPath<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>nextSibling<span class="token operator">?.</span>value<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// &quot;file2&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> previousSibling <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getPreviousSibling</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>indexPath<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>previousSibling<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// undefined (no previous sibling)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Get all siblings</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> siblings <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getSiblingNodes</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>indexPath<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>siblings<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">map</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>n<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> n<span class="token punctuation">.</span>value<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// [&quot;file1&quot;, &quot;file2&quot;]</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="index-path-operations" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Index Path Operations<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#index-path-operations"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Work with index paths to identify node positions:</p>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Get index path for a value</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> indexPath <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getIndexPath</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;file3&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>indexPath<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// [1, 0, 0]</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Get value from index path</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> value <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getValue</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>value<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// &quot;file3&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Get full value path (all ancestors + node)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> valuePath <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getValuePath</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>valuePath<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// [&quot;folder2&quot;, &quot;subfolder1&quot;, &quot;file3&quot;]</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Get node at specific index path</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> node <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">at</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>node<span class="token operator">?.</span>value<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// &quot;subfolder1&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="tree-queries" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Tree Queries<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#tree-queries"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<h4 id="branch-and-leaf-detection" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Branch and Leaf Detection<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#branch-and-leaf-detection"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Check if a node is a branch (has children)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> folder1Node <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">findNode</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;folder1&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> isBranch <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">isBranchNode</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>folder1Node<span class="token operator">!</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>isBranch<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// true</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Get all branch values</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> branchValues <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getBranchValues</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>branchValues<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// [&quot;folder1&quot;, &quot;folder2&quot;, &quot;subfolder1&quot;]</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="tree-traversal" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Tree Traversal<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#tree-traversal"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>Visit all nodes with custom logic:</p>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">visit</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">onEnter</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>node<span class="token punctuation">,</span> indexPath<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token string">Visiting: </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>node<span class="token punctuation">.</span>value<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string"> at depth </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>indexPath<span class="token punctuation">.</span>length<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// Skip certain branches</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>node<span class="token punctuation">.</span>value <span class="token operator">===</span> <span class="token string">&quot;folder2&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token string">&quot;skip&quot;</span> <span class="token comment">// Skip this branch and its children</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="filtering" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Filtering<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#filtering"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>Create a new tree with filtered nodes:</p>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Keep only nodes that match criteria</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> filteredTree <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">filter</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>node<span class="token punctuation">,</span> indexPath<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token keyword">return</span> node<span class="token punctuation">.</span>value<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">includes</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;file&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// Only keep files</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>filteredTree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getValues</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// [&quot;file1&quot;, &quot;file2&quot;, &quot;file3&quot;]</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="tree-manipulation" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Tree Manipulation<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#tree-manipulation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<h4 id="adding-nodes" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Adding Nodes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#adding-nodes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> newFile <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> value<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;newfile&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> label<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;New File.txt&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Insert after a specific node</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> indexPath <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getIndexPath</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;file1&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> updatedTree <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">insertAfter</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>indexPath<span class="token operator">!</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>newFile<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Insert before a specific node</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> updatedTree2 <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">insertBefore</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>indexPath<span class="token operator">!</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>newFile<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="removing-nodes" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Removing Nodes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#removing-nodes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> indexPath <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getIndexPath</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;file2&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> updatedTree <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">remove</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>indexPath<span class="token operator">!</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>updatedTree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getValues</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// file2 is removed</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="moving-nodes" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Moving Nodes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#moving-nodes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> fromIndexPaths <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getIndexPath</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;file1&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token operator">!</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> toIndexPath <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getIndexPath</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;folder2&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token operator">!</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> updatedTree <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">move</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fromIndexPaths<span class="token punctuation">,</span> toIndexPath<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// file1 is now moved under folder2</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="replacing-nodes" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Replacing Nodes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#replacing-nodes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> indexPath <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getIndexPath</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;file1&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token operator">!</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> newNode <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> value<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;replacedfile&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> label<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Replaced File.txt&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> updatedTree <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">replace</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>indexPath<span class="token punctuation">,</span> newNode<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="utility-methods" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Utility Methods<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#utility-methods"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<h4 id="flattening" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Flattening<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#flattening"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>Convert the tree to a flat structure:</p>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> flatNodes <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">flatten</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  flatNodes<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">map</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>n<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> value<span class="token operator">:</span> n<span class="token punctuation">.</span>value<span class="token punctuation">,</span> depth<span class="token operator">:</span> n<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_indexPath<span class="token punctuation">.</span>length <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// [{ value: &quot;folder1&quot;, depth: 1 }, { value: &quot;file1&quot;, depth: 2 }, ...]</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="getting-all-values" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Getting All Values<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#getting-all-values"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> allValues <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getValues</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>allValues<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// [&quot;folder1&quot;, &quot;file1&quot;, &quot;file2&quot;, &quot;folder2&quot;, &quot;subfolder1&quot;, &quot;file3&quot;]</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="depth-calculation" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Depth Calculation<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#depth-calculation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> depth <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getDepth</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;file3&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>depth<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// 3 (root -&gt; folder2 -&gt; subfolder1 -&gt; file3)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="working-with-custom-node-types" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Working with Custom Node Types<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#working-with-custom-node-types"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>You can customize how the tree collection interprets your data:</p>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">interface</span> <span class="token class-name">CustomNode</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  id<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token builtin">string</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  name<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token builtin">string</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  items<span class="token operator">?</span><span class="token operator">:</span> CustomNode<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  isDisabled<span class="token operator">?</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token builtin">boolean</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> customTree <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">TreeCollection<span class="token operator">&lt;</span>CustomNode<span class="token operator">&gt;</span></span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  rootNode<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    id<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    name<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    items<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token punctuation">{</span> id<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;1&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> name<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Item 1&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> isDisabled<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token punctuation">{</span> id<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;2&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> name<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Item 2&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> isDisabled<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">nodeToValue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>node<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> node<span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">nodeToString</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>node<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> node<span class="token punctuation">.</span>name<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">nodeToChildren</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>node<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> node<span class="token punctuation">.</span>items<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">isNodeDisabled</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>node<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> node<span class="token punctuation">.</span>isDisabled <span class="token operator">??</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="creating-trees-from-file-paths" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Creating Trees from File Paths<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#creating-trees-from-file-paths"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Create a tree structure from file paths:</p>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> filePathToTree <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/collection&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> paths <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token string">&quot;src/components/Button.tsx&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token string">&quot;src/components/Input.tsx&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token string">&quot;src/utils/helpers.ts&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token string">&quot;docs/README.md&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> fileTree <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">filePathToTree</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>paths<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileTree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getBranchValues</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// [&quot;src&quot;, &quot;components&quot;, &quot;utils&quot;, &quot;docs&quot;]</span>
</span></div></pre>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p><strong>Good to know</strong>: Tree collections are immutable - all modification methods
return a new tree instance rather than modifying the original.</p>

Collection class is designed to manage a collection of items, providing\nfunctionalities such as sorting, searching, getting next or previous items,\nconverting items to values or strings, checking if an item is disabled, and\nmore.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eGood to know\u003c/strong\u003e: This is used in the select and combobox components\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eList Collection\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eA list collection is a collection that is based on an array of items. It is\ncreated by passing an array of items to the constructor.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-ts\"\u003eimport { ListCollection } from \"@zag-js/collection\"\n\nconst ],\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eConverting value to item\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYou can convert a value to an item by passing the value to the \u003ccode\u003efind\u003c/code\u003e or\n\u003ccode\u003efindMany\u003c/code\u003e method.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-ts\"\u003econst item = collection.find(\"banana\")\n\nconsole.log(item) // { label: \"Banana\", value: \"banana\" }\n\nconst items = collection.findMany([\"apple\", \"banana\"])\n\nconsole.log(items) // [{ label: \"Apple\", value: \"apple\" }, { label: \"Banana\", value: \"banana\" }]\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eValue Traversal\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYou can get the next or previous item based on a value by passing the value to\nthe \u003ccode\u003egetNextValue\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003egetPreviousValue\u003c/code\u003e method.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-ts\"\u003econst nextValue = collection.getNextValue(\"apple\")\n\nconsole.log(nextValue) // banana\n\nconst previousItem = collection.getPreviousValue(\"banana\")\n\nconsole.log(previousItem) // apple\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eLikewise, you can also get the first or last item by calling the \u003ccode\u003efirstValue\u003c/code\u003e or\n\u003ccode\u003elastValue\u003c/code\u003e computed properties.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-ts\"\u003econsole.log(collection.firstValue) // apple\n\nconsole.log(collection.lastValue) // banana\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eCheck for value existence\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYou can check if a value exists in the collection by calling the \u003ccode\u003ehas\u003c/code\u003e method.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-ts\"\u003econst hasValue = collection.has(\"apple\")\n\nconsole.log(hasValue) // true\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eWorking with custom objects\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIf you are working with custom objects, you can pass a function to the\n\u003ccode\u003eitemToString\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003egetItemValue\u003c/code\u003e options to specify how to convert an item to a\nstring and a value, respectively.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-ts\"\u003eimport { ListCollection } from \"@zag-js/collection\"\n\nconst collection = new ListCollection({\n  items: [\n    { id: 1, name: \"apple\" },\n    { id: 2, name: \"banana\" },\n    { id: 3, name: \"cherry\" },\n  ],\n  itemToString: (item) =\u003e item.name,\n  itemToValue: (item) =\u003e item.id,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo disable an item, you can pass a function to the \u003ccode\u003eisItemDisabled\u003c/code\u003e option.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-ts\"\u003eimport { ListCollection } from \"@zag-js/collection\"\n\nconst collection = new ListCollection({\n  items: [\n    { id: 1, name: \"apple\" },\n    { id: 2, name: \"banana\" },\n    { id: 3, name: \"cherry\" },\n  ],\n  isItemDisabled: (item) =\u003e item.id === 2,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eReorder items\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYou can reorder items by calling the \u003ccode\u003ereorder\u003c/code\u003e method and passing the starting\nindex and the ending index of the item to be moved.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-ts\"\u003econst fromIndex = 1 // Banana\nconst toIndex = 0 // Apple\ncollection.reorder(fromIndex, toIndex)\n\nconsole.log(collection.items) // [{ label: \"Banana\", value: \"banana\" }, { label: \"Apple\", value: \"apple\" }]\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eTree Collection\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eA tree collection is designed to manage hierarchical data structures like file\nsystems, navigation menus, or organization charts. It provides powerful methods\nfor traversing, manipulating, and querying tree structures.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-ts\"\u003eimport { TreeCollection } from \"@zag-js/collection\"\n\nconst treeData = {\n  value: \"root\",\n  label: \"Root\",\n  children: [\n    {\n      value: \"folder1\",\n      label: \"Folder 1\",\n      children: [\n        { value: \"file1\", label: \"File 1.txt\" },\n        { value: \"file2\", label: \"File 2.txt\" },\n      ],\n    },\n    {\n      value: \"folder2\",\n      label: \"Folder 2\",\n      children: [\n        {\n          value: \"subfolder1\",\n          label: \"Subfolder 1\",\n          children: [{ value: \"file3\", label: \"File 3.txt\" }],\n        },\n      ],\n    },\n  ],\n}\n\nconst tree = new TreeCollection({ rootNode: treeData })\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eNavigation Methods\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe tree collection provides various methods to navigate through the\nhierarchical structure.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eGetting First and Last Nodes\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-ts\"\u003econst firstNode = n.value)) // [\"folder2\", \"subfolder1\"]\n\n// Get all descendant nodes\nconst descendants = tree.getDescendantNodes(\"folder1\")\nconsole.log(descendants.map((n) =\u003e n.value)) // [\"file1\", \"file2\"]\n\n// Get descendant values only\nconst descendantValues = tree.getDescendantValues(\"folder2\")\nconsole.log(descendantValues) // [\"subfolder1\", \"file3\"]\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eSibling Navigation\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eNavigate between sibling nodes:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-ts\"\u003e// Assuming we have the index path of \"file1\"\nconst indexPath = tree.getIndexPath(\"file1\") // [0, 0]\n\nconst nextSibling = tree.getNextSibling(indexPath)\nconsole.log(nextSibling?.value) // \"file2\"\n\nconst previousSibling = tree.getPreviousSibling(indexPath)\nconsole.log(previousSibling) // undefined (no previous sibling)\n\n// Get all siblings\nconst siblings = tree.getSiblingNodes(indexPath)\nconsole.log(siblings.map((n) =\u003e n.value)) // [\"file1\", \"file2\"]\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eIndex Path Operations\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWork with index paths to identify node positions:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-ts\"\u003e// Get index path for a value\nconst indexPath = tree.getIndexPath(\"file3\")\nconsole.log(indexPath) // [1, 0, 0]\n\n// Get value from index path\nconst value = tree.getValue([1, 0, 0])\nconsole.log(value) // \"file3\"\n\n// Get full value path (all ancestors + node)\nconst valuePath = tree.getValuePath([1, 0, 0])\nconsole.log(valuePath) // [\"folder2\", \"subfolder1\", \"file3\"]\n\n// Get node at specific index path\nconst node = tree.at([1, 0])\nconsole.log(node?.value) // \"subfolder1\"\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eTree Queries\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eBranch and Leaf Detection\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-ts\"\u003e// Check if a node is a branch (has children)\nconst folder1Node = tree.findNode(\"folder1\")\nconst isBranch = tree.isBranchNode(folder1Node!)\nconsole.log(isBranch) // true\n\n// Get all branch values\nconst branchValues = tree.getBranchValues()\nconsole.log(branchValues) // [\"folder1\", \"folder2\", \"subfolder1\"]\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eTree Traversal\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eVisit all nodes with custom logic:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-ts\"\u003etree.visit({\n  onEnter: (node, indexPath) =\u003e {\n    console.log(`Visiting: ${node.value} at depth ${indexPath.length}`)\n\n    // Skip certain branches\n    if (node.value === \"folder2\") {\n      return \"skip\" // Skip this branch and its children\n    }\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eFiltering\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eCreate a new tree with filtered nodes:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode Types\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYou can customize how the tree collection interprets your data:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-ts\"\u003einterface CustomNode {\n  id:
